msg:I was in Jiaxing and I booked this hotel with my dog â€‹â€‹because it was pet-friendly. I would like to share my experience here.
The pet room is located in the corner at the end of the corridor on the first floor, with a small door next to it for pets to enter and exit. The room was renovated from a basic room. Although the location is remote and the lighting is not good, for the pet owner, the fact that a high-star hotel can accept pets is itself a kind of progress and should be encouraged, so I will give it a five-star rating. I also hope that more comfortable rooms can be opened in the future for pet owners to choose.
In terms of facilities, the hotel also provides pet mats, towels, toilets, water basins and other supplies. Although we did not use them (we brought our own pet supplies), we can also feel that the hotel is very attentive to provide personalized services.
In addition, the hotel also requires that pets cannot land in public places, and provides pet strollers of different sizes. Our golden retriever weighing more than 60 kilograms can use a large stroller without any pressure.
Finally, thank you for the small gift given when leaving the hotel.

After several comparisons, I chose this hotel. Let me talk about my needs.
Eat well and sleep well, the hotel is clean and spacious, the fitness and swimming facilities are good, and the surrounding environment is elegant and comfortable. After the experience, I am quite satisfied. It can be said that it meets or even exceeds my expectations!
1. The hotel is a garden hotel. It covers a large area and combines Chinese and Western styles. It is spacious and bright. The lobby has a craft bar, reading area, cake afternoon tea, and self-service tea...
2. There are abundant food and beverages, including Western buffet and Chinese restaurant. Special praise for the environment and taste of the Chinese restaurant. The breakfast buffet is rich in variety and has everything you need, especially the bowl of lard Yangchun noodles, which is the best.
3. The environment is neat and clean, surrounded by park green space and surrounding the hotel. Not far next door is Xiuhu Park, which is quite beautiful and suitable for running enthusiasts.
4. The staff has a strong sense of service. They greet us with smiles and are very polite. Especially the freshly baked cookies, which are delicious. Before leaving, my son asked the front desk for another piece. A family of three prepares six bottles of Nongfu Spring.

msg:The hotel is large and resort style. There is a big lawn. The room size is okay, the bed is very comfortable, and the decoration is veteran style.

It also takes about 30 minutes to drive to major scenic spots such as Nanhu Lake, and 20 minutes to Yuehe River. I donâ€™t think itâ€™s a one-way trip, but the round trip only takes an hour, which is still quite time-consuming. There are not many restaurants around, so if you donâ€™t eat at the hotel, you have to drive out. A road goes back and forth N times.
The hotel has a water bus terminal that can go to an ancient town. However, it takes an hour one way and 2 hours round trip. Forget it.
The breakfast is very rich, both Chinese and Western snacks are delicious! There are also local specialty rice dumplings.
